**GT:** `7.723*epsilon**3 + 36.659*epsilon**0.2144*exp(-82.437/(8.314*T)) + epsilon*1.336*(T - 327.264)**2`

Let me expand the last term:
`epsilon*1.336*(T - 327.264)**2 = epsilon*1.336*(T² - 654.529*T + 107,102.0) = 1.336*epsilon*T² - 874.85*epsilon*T + 143,088*epsilon`

So GT has these basis functions:
- `epsilon**3` (pure polynomial in epsilon)
- `epsilon**0.2144 * exp(-c/T)` (fractional power of epsilon times Arrhenius-type term in T)
- `epsilon * T²` (cross term)
- `epsilon * T` (cross term)
- `epsilon` (linear in epsilon)

This is a complex expression with:
1. A cubic term in epsilon
2. A fractional power of epsilon times an exponential in 1/T
3. Quadratic dependence on T multiplied by epsilon

Let me check each candidate for the presence of these basis functions.

**Key observations about GT structure:**
- Contains `epsilon*T²` - quadratic in T
- Contains `epsilon^0.2144` - fractional power
- Contains `exp(-c/T)` - Arrhenius term
- Contains `epsilon^3` - cubic term

Most candidates have structures like `T*f(epsilon) + g(epsilon)` which is at most linear in T. The GT requires **quadratic** dependence on T (through the `epsilon*(T-c)²` term), so candidates that are only linear in T cannot match unless they have a `T²` term somehow.

Let me scan for candidates with T² or (T-c)² dependence:

- Candidates 1-31, 33-47, 50: Most have terms linear in T (like `T*c0`, `T*f(epsilon)`) but no T² terms.
- Candidate 32: Has `T**c2` which could give T² if c2=2, plus `c9/T**5` (extra term, can set c9=0). Let me check: `T*c0*exp(c1*epsilon) + T**c2*c3*sin(c4*epsilon+c5) + c6*epsilon**2 + c7*exp(c8*epsilon) + c9/T**5`. With c2=2: `T²*c3*sin(...)` - but sin can't produce epsilon^0.2144 or epsilon^3.
- Candidate 34: `T*c0*exp(c1*epsilon) + T*c2 + T**c3*c4*epsilon**c5 + c6*epsilon**2 + c7*exp(c8*epsilon)`. Has `T**c3*epsilon**c5` which could give T²*epsilon if c3=2, c5=1. But needs exp(-c/T) and epsilon^3 and epsilon^0.2144 - doesn't have them.
- Candidate 48: `T*c0*exp(c1*epsilon) + T**c2*c3*exp(c4*epsilon) + c5*epsilon**2 + c6*exp(c7*epsilon) + c8/T**5` - no T² * epsilon term possible.
- Candidate 49: `T*c0*epsilon**2 + T*c1*exp(c2*epsilon) + T**c3*c4*exp(c5*epsilon) + c6*epsilon**2 + c7*exp(c2*epsilon)` - no T²*epsilon.
- Candidate 13: `T**c5*c6*epsilon` - could give T²*epsilon if c5=2. But still needs epsilon^3, epsilon^0.2144*exp(-c/T).

None of the candidates have the right combination of:
1. `epsilon^3` (or equivalent)
2. `epsilon^(fractional) * exp(-c/T)` 
3. `epsilon * T²`

All candidates use exponentials in epsilon (`exp(c*epsilon)`) or sin/log functions, none of which can produce `epsilon^3` or `epsilon^0.2144` exactly. And almost none have the required T² dependence.

After careful analysis, **no candidate** can match the GT.
